function AttemptTeleport()
    task.spawn(function()
        repeat
            task.wait(3)

            local v9, _ = pcall(function()
                _TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, game.JobId, _LocalPlayer)
            end)
        until v9
    end)
end
function CheckKick(p10)
    if p10.Name == 'ErrorPrompt' then
        if p10.Visible and p10.TitleFrame.ErrorTitle.Text ~= 'Teleport Failed' then
            AttemptTeleport()
        end

        p10:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Visible'):Connect(function()
            if p10.Visible and p10.TitleFrame.ErrorTitle.Text ~= 'Teleport Failed' then
                AttemptTeleport()
            end
        end)
    end
end

_CoreGui.RobloxPromptGui.promptOverlay.ChildAdded:Connect(CheckKick)

        function u28.Kill(p36, p37)
            if p36 and p37 then
                if not p36:GetAttribute('Locked') then
                    p36:SetAttribute('Locked', p36.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)
                end

                PosMon = p36:GetAttribute('Locked').Position

                BringEnemy()
                EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)

                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool').ToolTip ~= 'Blox Fruit' then
                    _tp(p36.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(180), 0))
                else
                    _tp(p36.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 10, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(90), 0))
                end
                if RandomCFrame then
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p36.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25))
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p36.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(25, 30, 0))
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p36.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0))
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p36.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25))
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p36.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0))
                end
            end
        end

        function statsSetings(p48, p49)
            if p48 == 'Melee' then
                if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Melee', p49)
                end
            elseif p48 == 'Defense' then
                if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Defense', p49)
                end
            elseif p48 == 'Sword' then
                if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Sword', p49)
                end
            elseif p48 == 'Gun' then
                if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Gun', p49)
                end
            elseif p48 == 'Devil' and plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Demon Fruit', p49)
            end
        end
        function BringEnemy()
            local v50, v51, v52 = workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()
            local v53 = nil
            local v54 = {}

            while true do
                local v55

                v52, v55 = v50(v51, v52)

                if v52 == nil then
                    break
                end

                local _Humanoid2 = v55:FindFirstChild('Humanoid')
                local _PrimaryPart = v55:FindFirstChild('PrimaryPart')

                if _Humanoid2 and (_Humanoid2.Health > 0 and (_PrimaryPart and (_PrimaryPart.Position - v53).Magnitude <= 1000)) then
                    table.insert(v54, v55)
                end
            end

            if #v54 ~= 0 and v53 then
                local _Position = v54[math.random(1, #v54)].PrimaryPart.Position
                local v59, v60, v61 = ipairs(v54)

                while true do
                    local v62

                    v61, v62 = v59(v60, v61)

                    if v61 == nil then
                        break
                    end

                    local _Humanoid3 = v62:FindFirstChild('Humanoid')
                    local _PrimaryPart2 = v62:FindFirstChild('PrimaryPart')

                    if _Humanoid3 and _PrimaryPart2 then
                        _PrimaryPart2.AssemblyLinearVelocity = (_Position - _PrimaryPart2.Position).Unit * 150
                        _PrimaryPart2.CanCollide = true
                        _Humanoid3.WalkSpeed = 0
                        _Humanoid3.JumpPower = 0

                        local _Animator = _Humanoid3:FindFirstChild('Animator')

                        if _Animator then
                            _Animator:Destroy()
                        end

                        plr.SimulationRadius = math.huge
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        function Useskills(p66, p67)
            if p66 == 'Melee' then
                weaponSc('Melee')

                if p67 == 'Z' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Z', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Z', false, game)
                elseif p67 == 'X' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'X', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'X', false, game)
                elseif p67 == 'C' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'C', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'C', false, game)
                end
            elseif p66 == 'Sword' then
                weaponSc('Sword')

                if p67 == 'Z' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Z', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Z', false, game)
                elseif p67 == 'X' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'X', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'X', false, game)
                end
            elseif p66 == 'Blox Fruit' then
                weaponSc('Blox Fruit')

                if p67 == 'Z' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Z', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Z', false, game)
                elseif p67 == 'X' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'X', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'X', false, game)
                elseif p67 == 'C' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'C', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'C', false, game)
                elseif p67 == 'V' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'V', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'V', false, game)
                end
            elseif p66 == 'Gun' then
                weaponSc('Gun')

                if p67 == 'Z' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Z', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Z', false, game)
                elseif p67 == 'X' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'X', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'X', false, game)
                end
            end
            if p66 == 'nil' and p67 == 'Y' then
                vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Y', false, game)
                vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Y', false, game)
            end
        end

        local ___namecall = v68.__namecall

        setreadonly(v68, false)

        v68.__namecall = newcclosure(function(...)
            local v70 = getnamecallmethod()
            local v71 = {...}

            if tostring(v70) ~= 'FireServer' or (tostring(v71[1]) ~= 'RemoteEvent' or (tostring(v71[2]) == 'true' or tostring(v71[2]) == 'false')) or (not _G.FarmMastery_G or SoulGuitar) and (not _G.FarmMastery_Dev and (not _G.FarmBlazeEM and (not _G.Prehis_Skills and (not _G.SeaBeast1 and (not _G.FishBoat and (not _G.PGB and (not _G.Leviathan1 and (not _G.Complete_Trials and (not _G.AimMethod or ABmethod ~= 'AimBots Skill')))))))) and (not _G.AimMethod or ABmethod ~= 'Auto Aimbots')) then
                return ___namecall(...)
            end

            v71[2] = MousePos

            return ___namecall(unpack(v71))
        end)

        function GetConnectionEnemies(p72)
            local v73, v74, v75 = pairs(replicated:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v76

                v75, v76 = v73(v74, v75)

                if v75 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v76:IsA('Model') and (typeof(p72) == 'table' and table.find(p72, v76.Name) or v76.Name == p72) and (v76:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and v76.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
                    return v76
                end
            end

            local v77 = next
            local v78, v79 = game.Workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()

            while true do
                local v80

                v79, v80 = v77(v78, v79)

                if v79 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v80:IsA('Model') and (typeof(p72) == 'table' and table.find(p72, v80.Name) or v80.Name == p72) and (v80:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and v80.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
                    return v80
                end
            end
        end
        function LowCpu()
            local v81 = game
            local _Workspace = v81.Workspace
            local _Lighting = v81.Lighting
            local _Terrain = _Workspace.Terrain

            _Terrain.WaterWaveSize = 0
            _Terrain.WaterWaveSpeed = 0
            _Terrain.WaterReflectance = 0
            _Terrain.WaterTransparency = 0
            _Lighting.GlobalShadows = false
            _Lighting.FogEnd = 9000000000
            _Lighting.Brightness = 0
            settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = 'Level01'

            local v85, v86, v87 = pairs(v81:GetDescendants())
            local v88 = true

            while true do
                local v89

                v87, v89 = v85(v86, v87)

                if v87 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v89:IsA('Part') or (v89:IsA('Union') or (v89:IsA('CornerWedgePart') or v89:IsA('TrussPart'))) then
                    v89.Material = 'Plastic'
                    v89.Reflectance = 0
                elseif v89:IsA('Decal') or v89:IsA('Texture') and v88 then
                    v89.Transparency = 1
                elseif v89:IsA('ParticleEmitter') or v89:IsA('Trail') then
                    v89.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0)
                elseif v89:IsA('Explosion') then
                    v89.BlastPressure = 1
                    v89.BlastRadius = 1
                elseif v89:IsA('Fire') or (v89:IsA('SpotLight') or (v89:IsA('Smoke') or v89:IsA('Sparkles'))) then
                    v89.Enabled = false
                elseif v89:IsA('MeshPart') then
                    v89.Material = 'Plastic'
                    v89.Reflectance = 0
                    v89.TextureID = 1.0385902758728955e16
                end
            end

            local v90, v91, v92 = pairs(_Lighting:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v93

                v92, v93 = v90(v91, v92)

                if v92 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v93:IsA('BlurEffect') or (v93:IsA('SunRaysEffect') or (v93:IsA('ColorCorrectionEffect') or (v93:IsA('BloomEffect') or v93:IsA('DepthOfFieldEffect')))) then
                    v93.Enabled = false
                end
            end
        end

        function getInfinity_Ability(p160, p161)
            if Root then
                if p160 == 'Soru' and p161 then
                    local v162 = next
                    local v163, v164 = getgc()

                    while true do
                        local v165

                        v164, v165 = v162(v163, v164)

                        if v164 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if plr.Character.Soru and (typeof(v165) == 'function' and getfenv(v165).script == plr.Character.Soru) then
                            local v166 = next
                            local v167, v168 = getupvalues(v165)

                            while true do
                                local v169

                                v168, v169 = v166(v167, v168)

                                if v168 == nil then
                                    break
                                end
                                if typeof(v169) == 'table' then
                                    repeat
                                        wait(Sec)

                                        v169.LastUse = 0
                                    until not p161 or plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                elseif p160 == 'Energy' and p161 then
                    plr.Character.Energy.Changed:connect(function()
                        if p161 then
                            plr.Character.Energy.Value = Energy
                        end
                    end)
                elseif p160 == 'Observation' and p161 then
                    plr.VisionRadius.Value = math.huge
                end
            end
        end
        function Hop()
            pcall(function()
                for v170 = math.random(1, math.random(40, 75)), 100 do
                    local v171 = replicated.__ServerBrowser:InvokeServer(v170)
                    local v172 = next
                    local v173 = nil

                    while true do
                        local v174

                        v173, v174 = v172(v171, v173)

                        if v173 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if tonumber(v174.Count) < 12 then
                            TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, v173)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end

        function _tp(p189)
            local _Character5 = plr.Character

            if _Character5 and _Character5:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') then
                local _HumanoidRootPart = _Character5.HumanoidRootPart
                local _Magnitude = (p189.Position - _HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                local v193 = TweenInfo.new(_Magnitude / 350, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                local u194 = game:GetService('TweenService'):Create(_Part, v193, {CFrame = p189})

                if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == true then
                    _Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(_Part.Position.X, p189.Y, _Part.Position.Z)
                    plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                end

                local v195 = World1 and {
                    Vector3.new(-4652, 872, -1754),
                    Vector3.new(-7895, 5547, -380),
                    Vector3.new(61164, 5, 1820),
                    Vector3.new(3865, 5, -1926),
                } or {}
                local v196 = World2 and {
                    Vector3.new(923, 125, 32853),
                    Vector3.new(-6509, 83, -133),
                } or v195
                local v197 = World3 and {
                    Vector3.new(3029, 2280, -7325),
                    Vector3.new(28286, 14897, 103),
                } or v196
                local _GetUnlockables = CommF_('GetUnlockables')

                if World2 and _GetUnlockables.FlamingoAccess then
                    table.insert(v197, Vector3.new(-289, 306, 600))
                    table.insert(v197, Vector3.new(2284, 15, 905))
                end
                if World3 and _GetUnlockables.DefeatedIndraTrueForm then
                    table.insert(v197, Vector3.new(-12471, 374, -7551))
                    table.insert(v197, Vector3.new(5661, 1013, -335))
                    table.insert(v197, Vector3.new(-5074, 314, -3153))
                end

                local v199, v200, v201 = pairs(v197)
                local v202 = nil

                while true do
                    local v203

                    v201, v203 = v199(v200, v201)

                    if v201 == nil then
                        break
                    end

                    local _Magnitude2 = (v203 - p189.Position).Magnitude

                    if _Magnitude2 < _Magnitude then
                        v202 = v203
                        _Magnitude = _Magnitude2
                    end
                end

                if v202 ~= Vector3.new(3029, 2280, -7325) then
                    if v202 then
                        CommF_('requestEntrance', v202)
                        task.wait()
                        CommF_('requestEntrance', v202)
                    end
                else
                    _Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(28286, 14897, 103)

                    CommF_('requestEntrance', Vector3.new(28286, 14897, 103))
                    task.wait(0.1)

                    _Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(28609, 14896, 105)
                    _HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(28609, 14896, 105)

                    task.wait(0.1)

                    _Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(3029, 2280, -7325)

                    for _ = 1, 3 do
                        CommF_('RaceV4Progress', 'TeleportBack')
                    end

                    task.wait(0.2)
                end
                if _HumanoidRootPart.Position.Y ~= p189.Position.Y then
                    _Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(_HumanoidRootPart.Position.X, p189.Position.Y, _HumanoidRootPart.Position.Z)
                    _HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(_HumanoidRootPart.Position.X, p189.Position.Y, _HumanoidRootPart.Position.Z)
                end

                u194:Play()
                task.spawn(function()
                    while u194.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do
                        if not shouldTween then
                            u194:Cancel()

                            break
                        end

                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

        function QuestBeta()
            QuestB()

            return {
                [0] = _G.FindBoss,
                [1] = bMon,
                [2] = Qdata,
                [3] = Qname,
                [4] = PosB,
            }
        end

        function MaterialMon()
            local _LocalPlayer4 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local _Character6 = _LocalPlayer4.Character

            if _Character6 then
                _Character6 = _LocalPlayer4.Character:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')
            end
            if _Character6 then
                function shouldRequestEntrance(p222, p223)
                    if p223 <= (_Character6.Position - p222).Magnitude then
                        replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('requestEntrance', p222)
                    end
                end

                if World1 then
                    if SelectMaterial ~= 'Angel Wings' then
                        if SelectMaterial ~= 'Leather + Scrap Metal' then
                            if SelectMaterial ~= 'Magma Ore' then
                                if SelectMaterial == 'Fish Tail' then
                                    MMon = {
                                        'Fishman Warrior',
                                        'Fishman Commando',
                                        'Fishman Lord',
                                    }
                                    MPos = CFrame.new(61123, 19, 1569)
                                    SP = 'Default'

                                    local v224 = Vector3.new(61163.8515625, 5.342342376709, 1819.7841796875)

                                    shouldRequestEntrance(v224, 17000)
                                end
                            else
                                MMon = {
                                    'Military Soldier',
                                    'Military Spy',
                                    'Magma Admiral',
                                }
                                MPos = CFrame.new(-5815, 84, 8820)
                                SP = 'Default'
                            end
                        else
                            MMon = {
                                'Brute',
                                'Pirate',
                            }
                            MPos = CFrame.new(-1145, 15, 4350)
                            SP = 'Default'
                        end
                    else
                        MMon = {
                            'Shanda',
                            'Royal Squad',
                            'Royal Soldier',
                            'Wysper',
                            'Thunder God',
                        }
                        MPos = CFrame.new(-4698, 845, -1912)
                        SP = 'Default'

                        local v225 = Vector3.new(-4607.82275, 872.54248, -1667.55688)

                        shouldRequestEntrance(v225, 10000)
                    end
                elseif World2 then
                    if SelectMaterial ~= 'Leather + Scrap Metal' then
                        if SelectMaterial ~= 'Magma Ore' then
                            if SelectMaterial ~= 'Ectoplasm' then
                                if SelectMaterial ~= 'Mystic Droplet' then
                                    if SelectMaterial ~= 'Radioactive Material' then
                                        if SelectMaterial == 'Vampire Fang' then
                                            MMon = {
                                                'Vampire',
                                            }
                                            MPos = CFrame.new(-6033, 7, -1317)
                                            SP = 'Default'
                                        end
                                    else
                                        MMon = {
                                            'Factory Staff',
                                        }
                                        MPos = CFrame.new(295, 73, -56)
                                        SP = 'Default'
                                    end
                                else
                                    MMon = {
                                        'Water Fighter',
                                    }
                                    MPos = CFrame.new(-3385, 239, -10542)
                                    SP = 'Default'
                                end
                            else
                                MMon = {
                                    'Ship Deckhand',
                                    'Ship Engineer',
                                    'Ship Steward',
                                    'Ship Officer',
                                }
                                MPos = CFrame.new(911.35827636719, 125.95812988281, 33159.5390625)
                                SP = 'Default'

                                local v226 = Vector3.new(61163.8515625, 5.342342376709, 1819.7841796875)

                                shouldRequestEntrance(v226, 18000)
                            end
                        else
                            MMon = {
                                'Magma Ninja',
                                'Lava Pirate',
                            }
                            MPos = CFrame.new(-5428, 78, -5959)
                            SP = 'Default'
                        end
                    else
                        MMon = {
                            'Marine Captain',
                        }
                        MPos = CFrame.new(-2010.5059814453, 73.001159667969, -3326.6208496094)
                        SP = 'Default'
                    end
                elseif World3 then
                    if SelectMaterial ~= 'Scrap Metal' then
                        if SelectMaterial ~= 'Fish Tail' then

        function QuestNeta()
            QuestCheck()

            return {
                Mon,
                Qdata,
                Qname,
                PosM,
                NameMon,
                PosQ,
            }
        end

            Title = 'Auto Farm Level',
            Description = '',
            Default = false,
        }):OnChanged(function(p230)
            _G.Level = p230
        end)
        spawn(function()
            while wait(Sec) do
                if _G.Level then
                    pcall(function()
                        local _Text = plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text

                        if not string.find(_Text, QuestNeta()[5]) then
                            replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AbandonQuest')
                        end
                        if plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false then
                            _tp(QuestNeta()[6])

                            if (Root.Position - QuestNeta()[6].Position).Magnitude <= 5 then
                                replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('StartQuest', QuestNeta()[3], QuestNeta()[2])
                            end
                        end
                        if plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == true then
                            if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild(QuestNeta()[1]) then
                                local v232, v233, v234 = pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

                                while true do
                                    local v235

                                    v234, v235 = v232(v233, v234)

                                    if v234 == nil then
                                        break
                                    end
                                    if u28.Alive(v235) and v235.Name == QuestNeta()[1] then
                                        if string.find(_Text, QuestNeta()[5]) then
                                            wait()
                                            u28.Kill(v235, _G.Level)

                                            if _G.Level and (v235.Humanoid.Health > 0 and (v235.Parent and plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible ~= false)) then
                                            end
                                        else
                                            replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AbandonQuest')
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            else
                                _tp(QuestNeta()[4])

                                if replicated:FindFirstChild(QuestNeta()[1]) then
                                    _tp(replicated:FindFirstChild(QuestNeta()[1]).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0))
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
        end)
        v229.Main:AddToggle('TravelDress', {
            Title = 'Auto Travel Dressrosa',

            Default = false,
        }):OnChanged(function(p236)

        spawn(function()
            while wait(Sec) do

                    if _G.TravelDres and plr.Data.Level.Value >= 700 then
                        if workspace.Map.Ice.Door.CanCollide ~= true or workspace.Map.Ice.Door.Transparency ~= 0 then
                            if workspace.Map.Ice.Door.CanCollide ~= false or workspace.Map.Ice.Door.Transparency ~= 1 then

                                local _SwanPirate = GetConnectionEnemies('Swan Pirate')

                                if _SwanPirate then
                                    pcall(function()
                                        repeat
                                            wait()
                                            u28.Kill(_SwanPirate, _G.AutoZou)
                                        until not _SwanPirate.Parent or (_SwanPirate.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or (_G.AutoZou == false or plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false))

                                while true do
                                    local v247

                                    v246, v247 = v244(v245, v246)

                                    if v246 == nil then
                                        break
                                    end

                                    local v248, v249, v250 = pairs(v247)

                                    while true do
                                        local v251

                                        v250, v251 = v248(v249, v250)

                                        if v250 == nil then
                                            break
                                        end
                                        if v250 == 'Name' then
                                            table.insert(TabelDevilFruitStore, v251)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end

                                local v252 = next
                                local _GetFruits, v254 = game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('Remotes').CommF_:InvokeServer('GetFruits')

        local u344 = {}

        local function u351(p345)
            local v346, v347, v348 = p345:GetChildren()

            while true do
                local v349

                v348, v349 = v346(v347, v348)

                if v348 == nil then
                    break
                end

                local _Humanoid5 = v349:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')

                if v349:GetAttribute('IsBoss') and (_Humanoid5 and _Humanoid5.Health > 0) then
                    table.insert(u344, v349.Name)
                end
            end
        end

        u351(workspace.Enemies)
        u351(game.ReplicatedStorage)
        table.sort(u344)

        function UpdateBossList()
            u344 = {}

            u351(workspace.Enemies)
            u351(game.ReplicatedStorage)
            table.sort(u344)
            DropBossList:SetValue(u344)
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            local v356 = nil

            while task.wait() do
                if _G.KillBoss and _G.SelectBoss ~= '' then
                    if v356 ~= _G.SelectBoss then
                        local _SelectBoss = _G.SelectBoss

                        spawn(function()
                            while true do
                                while true do
                                    if not _G.KillBoss or _SelectBoss ~= _G.SelectBoss then
                                        return
                                    end

                                    local _PlayerGui = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild('PlayerGui')

                                    if _PlayerGui then
                                        _PlayerGui = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild('Main')
                                    end
                                    if _PlayerGui then
                                        _PlayerGui = _PlayerGui:FindFirstChild('Quest')
                                    end
                                    if _PlayerGui then
                                        _PlayerGui = _PlayerGui:FindFirstChild('Title')
                                    end
                                    if _PlayerGui then
                                        _PlayerGui = _PlayerGui:FindFirstChild('Text')
                                    end
                                    if _PlayerGui and not _PlayerGui:find(_G.SelectBoss) then
                                        CommF_('AbandonQuest')
                                    end

                                    local _Enemies = workspace:FindFirstChild('Enemies')
                                    local _ReplicatedStorage2 = game.ReplicatedStorage
                                    local v361 = _Enemies and _Enemies:FindFirstChild(_G.SelectBoss)

                                    if v361 then
                                        _ReplicatedStorage2 = v361
                                    elseif _ReplicatedStorage2 then
                                        _ReplicatedStorage2 = _ReplicatedStorage2:FindFirstChild(_G.SelectBoss)
                                    end

                                    local v362 = GetBossQuest(_G.SelectBoss)

                                    if v362 and (typeof(v362[1]) == 'string' and (typeof(v362[2]) == 'number' and typeof(v362[3]) == 'number')) then
                                        local v363 = plr and plr:FindFirstChild('Data')

                                        if v363 then
                                            v363 = plr.Data:FindFirstChild('Level')
                                        end
                                        if v363 and v363.Value >= v362[3] then
                                            CommF_('StartQuest', v362[1], v362[2])
                                        end
                                    end
                                    if _ReplicatedStorage2 and (_ReplicatedStorage2:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (_ReplicatedStorage2:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and _ReplicatedStorage2.Humanoid.Health > 0)) then
                                        break
                                    end

                                    task.wait(1)
                                end

                                task.wait()
                                u28.Kill(_ReplicatedStorage2, _G.KillBoss)

                                if _ReplicatedStorage2.Humanoid.Health > 0 and (_G.KillBoss and _G.SelectBoss == _SelectBoss) then
                                end
                            end
                        end)

                        v356 = _SelectBoss
                    end
                else
                    v356 = nil
                end
            end
        end)
        task.spawn(function()
            while true do
                while true do
                    repeat
                        if not task.wait() then
                            return
                        end
                    until _G.KillAllBosses

                    local _Character7 = plr.Character

                    if not (_Character7 and _Character7:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')) then
                        return
                    end

                    local _HumanoidRootPart3 = _Character7.HumanoidRootPart
                    local v366 = nil
                    local _huge2 = math.huge
                    local _Enemies2 = workspace:FindFirstChild('Enemies')

                    if _Enemies2 then
                        local v369, v370, v371 = _Enemies2:GetChildren()

                        while true do
                            local v372

                            v371, v372 = v369(v370, v371)

                            if v371 == nil then
                                break
                            end

                            local _Humanoid6 = v372:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')
                            local _HumanoidRootPart4 = v372:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')

                            if v372:GetAttribute('IsBoss') and (_Humanoid6 and (_Humanoid6.Health > 0 and _HumanoidRootPart4)) then
                                local _Magnitude4 = (_HumanoidRootPart4.Position - _HumanoidRootPart3.Position).Magnitude

                                if _Magnitude4 < _huge2 then
                                    _huge2 = _Magnitude4
                                    v366 = v372
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if not v366 then
                        local v376, v377, v378 = game.ReplicatedStorage:GetChildren()

                        while true do
                            local v379

                            v378, v379 = v376(v377, v378)

                            if v378 == nil then
                                break
                            end

                            local _Humanoid7 = v379:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')
                            local v381 = v379:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') or (v379:FindFirstChild('PrimaryPart') or v379:FindFirstChild('Handle'))

                            if v379:GetAttribute('IsBoss') and (_Humanoid7 and (_Humanoid7.Health > 0 and v381)) then
                                local _Magnitude5 = (v381.Position - _HumanoidRootPart3.Position).Magnitude

                                if _Magnitude5 < _huge2 then
                                    _tp(CFrame.new(v381.Position + Vector3.new(0, 30, 0)))

                                    _huge2 = _Magnitude5
                                    v366 = v379
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if v366 then
                        break
                    end

                    task.wait(1)
                end

                local _Humanoid8 = v366:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')

                if _Humanoid8 and (_Humanoid8.Health > 0 and v366:IsDescendantOf(workspace.Enemies)) then
                    u28.Kill(v366, _G.KillAllBosses)
                end

                task.wait()

                if v366:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid') and (v366.Humanoid.Health > 0 and _G.KillAllBosses) then
                    break
                end
            end
        end)

        function AuraSkin(p499)
            local v500 = {
                {
                    StorageName = p499,
                    Type = 'AuraSkin',
                    Context = 'Equip',
                },
            }

            replicated:WaitForChild('Modules'):WaitForChild('Net'):WaitForChild('RF/FruitCustomizerRF'):InvokeServer(unpack(v500))
        end
        function VaildColor(p501)
            if p501 and p501.BrickColor then
                return tostring(p501.BrickColor) == 'Lime green'
            end
        end
        function HakiCalculate(p502)
            local v503 = {
                ['Really red'] = 'Pure Red',
                Oyster = 'Snow White',
                ['Hot pink'] = 'Winter Sky',
            }

            if p502 and p502.BrickColor then
                return v503[tostring(p502.BrickColor)]
            end
        end

                            local v505, v506, v507 = pairs(_Summoner:FindFirstChild('Circle'):GetChildren())

                            while true do
                                local v508

                                    break

                                    local _Part2 = v508:FindFirstChild('Part')

        function getT(p765)
            local v766 = nil

            if p765 == 1 then
                v766 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment1.Line.Rotation
            elseif p765 == 3 then
                v766 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment3.Line.Rotation
            elseif p765 == 4 then
                v766 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment4.Line.Rotation
            elseif p765 == 7 then
                v766 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment7.Line.Rotation
            elseif p765 == 10 then
                v766 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment10.Line.Rotation
            end
            if v766 then
                return v766.Z
            end
        end
        function getRT(p767)
            local _Quest4 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Trophies.Quest
            local v769, v770, v771 = pairs(_Quest4:GetChildren())
            local v772 = nil

            while true do
                local v773

                v771, v773 = v769(v770, v771)

                if v771 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if p767 == 1 and (v773.Name == 'Trophy1' and v773:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                    v772 = v773.Handle.Rotation
                elseif p767 == 2 and (v773.Name == 'Trophy2' and v773:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                    v772 = v773.Handle.Rotation
                elseif p767 == 3 and (v773.Name == 'Trophy3' and v773:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                    v772 = v773.Handle.Rotation
                elseif p767 == 4 and (v773.Name == 'Trophy4' and v773:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                    v772 = v773.Handle.Rotation
                elseif p767 == 5 and (v773.Name == 'Trophy5' and v773:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                    v772 = v773.Handle.Rotation
                end
                if v772 then
                    return v772.Z
                end
            end
        end

                    if _G.AutoMatSoul and GetWP('Skull Guitar') == false then
                        if GetM('Bones') < 500 or (GetM('Ectoplasm') < 250 or GetM('Dark Fragment') < 1) then
                            if GetM('Ectoplasm') > 250 then
                                if GetM('Dark Fragment') >= 1 then
                                    if GetM('Bones') <= 500 then

                                                'Reborn Skeleton',
                                                'Living Zombie',

                                            })

                                                repeat

                                                    u28.Kill(v788, _G.AutoMatSoul)
                                                until not _G.AutoMatSoul or (v788.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or (not v788.Parent or v788.Humanoid.Health <= 0))
                                            else
                                                _tp(CFrame.new(-9504.8564453125, 172.14292907715, 6057.259765625))
                                            end
                                        else
                                            replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('TravelZou')
                                        end
                                    end

        function GetSeaBeastTrial()
            if not workspace.Map:FindFirstChild('FishmanTrial') then
                return nil
            end
            if workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Trial of Water') then
                FishmanTrial = workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Trial of Water')
            end
            if FishmanTrial then
                local v803 = next
                local v804, v805 = workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren()

                while true do
                    local v806

                    v805, v806 = v803(v804, v805)

                    if v805 == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if v806:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and ((v806.HumanoidRootPart.Position - FishmanTrial.Position).Magnitude <= 1500 and v806.Health.Value > 0) then
                        return v806
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        spawn(function()
            while wait(Sec) do
                pcall(function()
                    if _G.Complete_Trials and tostring(plr.Data.Race.Value) == 'Mink' then
                        notween(workspace.Map.MinkTrial.Ceiling.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -20, 0))
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)
        spawn(function()
            while wait(Sec) do
                pcall(function()
                    if _G.Complete_Trials and (tostring(plr.Data.Race.Value) == 'Fishman' and GetSeaBeastTrial()) then
                        repeat
                            task.wait()
                            spawn(function()
                                _tp(CFrame.new(GetSeaBeastTrial().HumanoidRootPart.Position.X, game:GetService('Workspace').Map['WaterBase-Plane'].Position.Y + 300, GetSeaBeastTrial().HumanoidRootPart.Position.Z))
                            end)

                            MousePos = GetSeaBeastTrial().HumanoidRootPart.Position

                            Useskills('Melee', 'Z')
                            Useskills('Melee', 'X')
                            Useskills('Melee', 'C')
                            wait(0.1)
                            Useskills('Sword', 'Z')
                            Useskills('Sword', 'X')
                            wait(0.1)
                            Useskills('Blox Fruit', 'Z')
                            Useskills('Blox Fruit', 'X')
                            Useskills('Blox Fruit', 'C')
                            wait(0.1)
                            Useskills('Gun', 'Z')
                            Useskills('Gun', 'X')
                        until _G.Complete_Trials == false or not GetSeaBeastTrial()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)
        spawn(function()
            while wait(Sec) do
                pcall(function()
                    if _G.Complete_Trials and tostring(plr.Data.Race.Value) == 'Cyborg' then
                        _tp(workspace.Map.CyborgTrial.Floor.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 500, 0))
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)
        spawn(function()
            while wait(Sec) do
                pcall(function()
                    if _G.Complete_Trials and tostring(plr.Data.Race.Value) == 'Skypiea' then
                        notween(workspace.Map.SkyTrial.Model.FinishPart.CFrame)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)

                        'Ancient Vampire',

        function isnil(p1044)
            return p1044 == nil
        end

        local function u1046(p1045)
            return math.floor(tonumber(p1045) + 0.5)
        end

        Number = math.random(1, 1000000)

        function EspPly()
            local v1047 = next
            local v1048, v1049 = game.Players:GetChildren()

            while true do
                local u1050

                v1049, u1050 = v1047(v1048, v1049)

                if v1049 == nil then
                    break
                end

                pcall(function()
                    if not isnil(u1050.Character) then
                        if PlayerEsp then
                            if u1050 == plr or isnil(u1050.Character.Head) or u1050.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number) then
                                u1050.Character.Head['NameEsp' .. Number].TextLabel.Text = u1050.Data.Level.Value .. ' | ' .. u1050.Name .. ' | ' .. u1046((game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position - u1050.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. ' M Health : ' .. u1046(u1050.Character.Humanoid.Health * 100 / u1050.Character.Humanoid.MaxHealth) .. '%'
                            else
                                local _BillboardGui = Instance.new('BillboardGui', u1050.Character.Head)

                                _BillboardGui.Name = 'NameEsp' .. Number
                                _BillboardGui.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
                                _BillboardGui.Size = UDim2.new(1, 200, 1, 30)
                                _BillboardGui.Adornee = u1050.Character.Head
                                _BillboardGui.AlwaysOnTop = true

                                local _TextLabel = Instance.new('TextLabel', _BillboardGui)

                                _TextLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Code
                                _TextLabel.FontSize = 'Size14'
                                _TextLabel.TextWrapped = true
                                _TextLabel.Text = u1050.Name .. ' ' .. u1046((game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position - u1050.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. ' M'
                                _TextLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                                _TextLabel.TextYAlignment = 'Top'
                                _TextLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                                _TextLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5

                                if u1050.Team ~= TeamSelf then
                                    _TextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.new(255, 0, 0)
                                else
                                    _TextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 254)
                                end
                            end
                        elseif u1050.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number) then
                            u1050.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number):Destroy()
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

        function DevEsp()
            local _Character10 = plr.Character

            if _Character10 then
                local _Head = _Character10:FindFirstChild('Head')

                if _Head then
                    if not DevilFruitESP then
                        local v1061, v1062, v1063 = pairs(workspace:GetChildren())

                        while true do
                            local v1064

                            v1063, v1064 = v1061(v1062, v1063)

                            if v1063 == nil then
                                break
                            end
                            if v1064.Name:lower():find('fruit') and v1064:FindFirstChild('Handle') and v1064.Handle:FindFirstChild('Fruit ESP') then
                                v1064.Handle['Fruit ESP']:Destroy()
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if DevilFruitESP then
                        local v1065, v1066, v1067 = pairs(workspace:GetChildren())

                        while true do
                            local v1068

                            v1067, v1068 = v1065(v1066, v1067)

                            if v1067 == nil then
                                break
                            end
                            if v1068.Name:find('Fruit') then
                                local _Fruit = v1068:FindFirstChild('Fruit')

                                if not _Fruit then
                                    return
                                end

                                local _Handle = v1068:FindFirstChild('Handle')

                                if not _Handle then
                                    return
                                end

                                local _Idle = _Fruit:FindFirstChild('Idle')
                                local _Animation = _Fruit:FindFirstChild('Animation')
                                local _Fruit2 = _Fruit:FindFirstChild('Fruit')
                                local v1074 = _Idle and _Idle.AnimationId or _Animation and _Animation.AnimationId

                                if v1074 then
                                    _Fruit2 = v1074
                                elseif _Fruit2 then
                                    _Fruit2 = _Fruit2.MeshId
                                end

                                local v1075 = FruitsData[_Fruit2]

                                if v1075 then
                                    local _Name = v1075.Name
                                    local _Image = v1075.Image
                                    local v1078 = RarityColor[v1075.Rarity]
                                    local v1079 = math.floor((_Handle.Position - _Head.Position).Magnitude / 5)
                                    local _fontcolorssfontfontcolorrgb120120120dfont = string.format("<font color='%s'>%s</font> <font color='rgb(120, 120, 120)'>[%d]</font>", v1078, _Name or '???', v1079)

                                    if _Handle:FindFirstChild('Fruit ESP') then
                                        _Handle['Fruit ESP'].Label.Text = _fontcolorssfontfontcolorrgb120120120dfont
                                    else
                                        local _BillboardGui3 = Instance.new('BillboardGui', _Handle)

                                        _BillboardGui3.Name = 'Fruit ESP'
                                        _BillboardGui3.Size = UDim2.new(0, 240, 0, 40)
                                        _BillboardGui3.Adornee = _Handle
                                        _BillboardGui3.AlwaysOnTop = true

                                        local _TextLabel3 = Instance.new('TextLabel', _BillboardGui3)

                                        _TextLabel3.Name = 'Label'
                                        _TextLabel3.Font = 'Code'
                                        _TextLabel3.TextSize = 14
                                        _TextLabel3.RichText = true
                                        _TextLabel3.Text = _fontcolorssfontfontcolorrgb120120120dfont
                                        _TextLabel3.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                                        _TextLabel3.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                                        _TextLabel3.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
                                        _TextLabel3.AutoLocalize = true

                                        local _ImageLabel = Instance.new('ImageLabel', _BillboardGui3)

                                        _ImageLabel.Name = 'Fruit Image'
                                        _ImageLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                                        _ImageLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 65, 0, 65)
                                        _ImageLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, -50)
                                        _ImageLabel.Image = _Image
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                return
            end
        end

        function LegenSword()
            if LegenS ~= true then
                if workspace:FindFirstChild('Lgd') then
                    workspace:FindFirstChild('Lgd'):Destroy()
                end
            else
                local v1114, v1115, v1116 = pairs(replicated.NPCs:GetChildren())

                while true do
                    local v1117

                    v1116, v1117 = v1114(v1115, v1116)

                    if v1116 == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if v1117.Name == 'Legendary Sword Dealer ' then
                        if workspace:FindFirstChild('Lgd') then
                            if workspace:FindFirstChild('Lgd') then
                                if Lgd:FindFirstChild('NameEsp') then
                                    Lgd.NameEsp.TextLabel.Text = v1117.Name .. ' ' .. u1046((plr.Character.Head.Position - v1117.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. ' M'
                                else
                                    local _BillboardGui9 = Instance.new('BillboardGui', Lgd)

                                    _BillboardGui9.Name = 'NameEsp'
                                    _BillboardGui9.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
                                    _BillboardGui9.Size = UDim2.new(1, 200, 1, 30)
                                    _BillboardGui9.Adornee = Lgd
                                    _BillboardGui9.AlwaysOnTop = true

                                    local _TextLabel9 = Instance.new('TextLabel', _BillboardGui9)

                                    _TextLabel9.Font = 'Code'
                                    _TextLabel9.FontSize = 'Size14'
                                    _TextLabel9.TextWrapped = true
                                    _TextLabel9.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                                    _TextLabel9.TextYAlignment = 'Top'
                                    _TextLabel9.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                                    _TextLabel9.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
                                    _TextLabel9.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 245, 245)
                                end
                            end
                        else
                            Lgd = Instance.new('Part')
                            Lgd.Name = 'Lgd'
                            Lgd.Transparency = 1
                            Lgd.Size = Vector3.new(1, 1, 1)
                            Lgd.Anchored = true
                            Lgd.CanCollide = false
                            Lgd.Parent = workspace
                            Lgd.CFrame = v1117.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        function ChestEsp()
            if ChestESP then
                local _CollectionService4 = game:GetService('CollectionService')
                local _LocalPlayer9 = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
                local _Position6 = (_LocalPlayer9.Character or _LocalPlayer9.CharacterAdded:Wait()):GetPivot().Position
                local __ChestTagged3 = _CollectionService4:GetTagged('_ChestTagged')
                local v1124, v1125, v1126 = ipairs(__ChestTagged3)

                while true do
                    local u1127

                    v1126, u1127 = v1124(v1125, v1126)

                    if v1126 == nil then
                        break
                    end

                    local v1128

                    if SelectedIsland and not u1127:IsDescendantOf(SelectedIsland) or u1127:GetAttribute('IsDisabled') then
                        v1128 = true
                    end

                    local v1129, v1130 = pcall(function()
                        return u1127:GetPivot().Position
                    end)

                    if not v1129 then
                        if not u1127:IsA('BasePart') then
                            v1128 = true
                        end

                        v1130 = u1127.Position
                    end

                    local _Magnitude8 = (v1130 - _Position6).Magnitude

                    u1127:GetFullName():gsub('[^%w_]', '_')

                    local _ChestEspAttachment = u1127:FindFirstChild('ChestEspAttachment')

                    if not _ChestEspAttachment then
                        local _Attachment = Instance.new('Attachment')

                        _Attachment.Name = 'ChestEspAttachment'
                        _Attachment.Parent = u1127
                        _Attachment.Position = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)

                        local _BillboardGui10 = Instance.new('BillboardGui')

                        _BillboardGui10.Name = 'NameEsp'
                        _BillboardGui10.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 30)
                        _BillboardGui10.Adornee = _Attachment
                        _BillboardGui10.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
                        _BillboardGui10.AlwaysOnTop = true
                        _BillboardGui10.Parent = _Attachment

                        local _TextLabel10 = Instance.new('TextLabel')

                        _TextLabel10.Font = Enum.Font.Code
                        _TextLabel10.TextSize = 14
                        _TextLabel10.TextWrapped = true
                        _TextLabel10.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                        _TextLabel10.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top
                        _TextLabel10.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                        _TextLabel10.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
                        _TextLabel10.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 245, 245)
                        _TextLabel10.Parent = _BillboardGui10
                    end

                    local v1136

                    if _ChestEspAttachment then
                        v1136 = _ChestEspAttachment:FindFirstChild('NameEsp')
                    else
                        v1136 = _ChestEspAttachment
                    end
                    if v1136 then
                        local v1137 = math.floor(_Magnitude8 / 3)
                        local _Label = u1127.Name:gsub('Label', '')

                        v1136.TextLabel.Text = string.format('[%s] %d M', _Label, v1137)
                    end
                    if _G_AutoFarmChest and (_Magnitude8 <= 20 and _ChestEspAttachment) then
                        _ChestEspAttachment:Destroy()

                        v1128 = true
                    else
                        v1128 = true
                    end
                    if not v1128 then
                        break
                    end
                end
            else
                local v1139, v1140, v1141 = ipairs(game:GetService('CollectionService'):GetTagged('_ChestTagged'))

                while true do
                    local v1142

                    v1141, v1142 = v1139(v1140, v1141)

                    if v1141 == nil then
                        break
                    end

                    local _ChestEspAttachment2 = v1142:FindFirstChild('ChestEspAttachment')

                    if _ChestEspAttachment2 then
                        _ChestEspAttachment2:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        function berriesEsp()

                    while true do

                        if v1154 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v1155 and (not BerryArray or table.find(BerryArray, v1155)) then

                                _BillboardGui11.Name = 'NameEsp'

                            if _G.AutoBerry and math.round(v1161) <= 20 then
                                v1157:Destroy()
                            end

                    end
                end

            Callback = function()
                local _HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService')
                local _TeleportService2 = game:GetService('TeleportService')
                local _PlaceId2 = game.PlaceId
                local u1237 = 'https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. _PlaceId2 .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100'

                function ListServers(p1238)
                    return _HttpService:JSONDecode((game:HttpGet(u1237 .. (p1238 and '&cursor=' .. p1238 or ''))))
                end

                local v1239 = nil

                repeat
                    local v1240 = ListServers(v1239)
                    local v1241 = v1240.data[1]

                    v1239 = v1240.nextPageCursor
                until v1241

                _TeleportService2:TeleportToPlaceInstance(_PlaceId2, v1241.id, plr)
            end,
        })
        v229.Misc:AddButton({
            Title = 'Hop to Lowest Pings Server',
            Description = '',
            Callback = function()
                local _HttpService2 = game:GetService('HttpService')
                local _TeleportService3 = game:GetService('TeleportService')
                local _Stats = game:GetService('Stats')

                local function v1250(p1245, p1246)
                    local _httpsgamesrobloxcomv1gamesdserversPubliclimitd = string.format('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/%d/servers/Public?limit=%d', p1245, p1246)
                    local v1248, v1249 = pcall(function()
                        return _HttpService2:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet(_httpsgamesrobloxcomv1gamesdserversPubliclimitd))
                    end)

                    if v1248 and (v1249 and v1249.data) then
                        return v1249.data
                    else
                        return nil
                    end
                end

                local _PlaceId3 = game.PlaceId
                local v1252 = v1250(_PlaceId3, 100)

                if v1252 then
                    local v1253 = v1252[1]
                    local v1254, v1255, v1256 = pairs(v1252)

                    while true do
                        local v1257

                        v1256, v1257 = v1254(v1255, v1256)

                        if v1256 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v1257.ping < v1253.ping then
                            if v1257.maxPlayers > v1257.playing then
                                v1253 = v1257
                            end
                        end
                    end

                    task.wait(0.5)

                    local v1258 = _Stats.Network.ServerStatsItem['Data Ping']:GetValueString()

                    if tonumber(v1258:match('(%d+)')) >= 100 then
                        _TeleportService3:TeleportToPlaceInstance(_PlaceId3, v1253.id)
                    end
                end
            end,
        })

        rtxM = v229.Misc:AddToggle('rtxM', {
            Title = 'Turn on RTX Mode',
            Description = '',
            Default = false,
        })

        rtxM:OnChanged(function(p1266)
            _G.RTXMode = p1266

            local _Lighting2 = game.Lighting
            local _ColorCorrectionEffect = Instance.new('ColorCorrectionEffect', _Lighting2)
            local _ColorCorrectionEffect2 = Instance.new('ColorCorrectionEffect', _Lighting2)

            OldAmbient = _Lighting2.Ambient
            OldBrightness = _Lighting2.Brightness
            OldColorShift_Top = _Lighting2.ColorShift_Top
            OldBrightnessc = _ColorCorrectionEffect.Brightness
            OldContrastc = _ColorCorrectionEffect.Contrast
            OldTintColorc = _ColorCorrectionEffect.TintColor
            OldTintColore = _ColorCorrectionEffect2.TintColor

            if _G.RTXMode then
                while _G.RTXMode do
                    wait()

                    _Lighting2.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(33, 33, 33)
                    _Lighting2.Brightness = 0.3
                    _ColorCorrectionEffect.Brightness = 0.176
                    _ColorCorrectionEffect.Contrast = 0.39
                    _ColorCorrectionEffect.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(217, 145, 57)
                    game.Lighting.FogEnd = 999

                    if not plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild('PointLight') then
                        local _PointLight = Instance.new('PointLight')

                        _PointLight.Parent = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                        _PointLight.Range = 15
                        _PointLight.Color = Color3.fromRGB(217, 145, 57)
                    end
                    if not _G.RTXMode then
                        _Lighting2.Ambient = OldAmbient
                        _Lighting2.Brightness = OldBrightness
                        _Lighting2.ColorShift_Top = OldColorShift_Top
                        _ColorCorrectionEffect.Contrast = OldContrastc
                        _ColorCorrectionEffect.Brightness = OldBrightnessc
                        _ColorCorrectionEffect.TintColor = OldTintColorc
                        _ColorCorrectionEffect2.TintColor = OldTintColore
                        game.Lighting.FogEnd = 2500

                        plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild('PointLight'):Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
        end)

        function AttackNoCoolDown()
            local _LocalPlayer12 = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
            local _Character12 = _LocalPlayer12.Character

            if not _Character12 then
                return
            end

            local v1325, v1326, v1327 = ipairs(_Character12:GetChildren())
            local v1328 = nil

            while true do
                local v1329

                v1327, v1329 = v1325(v1326, v1327)

                if v1327 == nil then
                    v1329 = v1328

                    break
                end
                if v1329:IsA('Tool') then
                    break
                end
            end

            if v1329 then
                local v1330 = u1322(_Character12, 60)

                if #v1330 ~= 0 then
                    local _ReplicatedStorage3 = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage')
                    local _Modules = _ReplicatedStorage3:FindFirstChild('Modules')

                    if _Modules then
                        local _RERegisterAttack = _ReplicatedStorage3:WaitForChild('Modules'):WaitForChild('Net'):WaitForChild('RE/RegisterAttack')
                        local _RERegisterHit = _ReplicatedStorage3:WaitForChild('Modules'):WaitForChild('Net'):WaitForChild('RE/RegisterHit')

                        if _RERegisterAttack and _RERegisterHit then
                            local v1335, v1336, v1337 = ipairs(v1330)
                            local v1338 = {}
                            local v1339 = nil

                            while true do
                                local v1340

                                v1337, v1340 = v1335(v1336, v1337)

                                if v1337 == nil then
                                    break
                                end
                                if not v1340:GetAttribute('IsBoat') then
                                    local v1341 = {
                                        'RightLowerArm',
                                        'RightUpperArm',
                                        'LeftLowerArm',
                                        'LeftUpperArm',
                                        'RightHand',
                                        'LeftHand',
                                    }
                                    local v1342 = v1340:FindFirstChild(v1341[math.random(#v1341)]) or v1340.PrimaryPart

                                    if v1342 then
                                        table.insert(v1338, {v1340, v1342})

                                        v1339 = v1342
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            if v1339 then
                                _RERegisterAttack:FireServer(0)

                                local _PlayerScripts = _LocalPlayer12:FindFirstChild('PlayerScripts')

                                if _PlayerScripts then
                                    local _LocalScript = _PlayerScripts:FindFirstChildOfClass('LocalScript')

                                    while not _LocalScript do
                                        _PlayerScripts.ChildAdded:Wait()

                                        _LocalScript = _PlayerScripts:FindFirstChildOfClass('LocalScript')
                                    end

                                    local v1345 = nil

                                    if getsenv then
                                        local v1346, v1347 = pcall(getsenv, _LocalScript)

                                        if v1346 and v1347 then
                                            v1345 = v1347._G.SendHitsToServer
                                        end
                                    end

                                    local v1348, v1349 = pcall(function()
                                        return require(_Modules.Flags).COMBAT_REMOTE_THREAD or false
                                    end)

                                    if v1348 and (v1349 and v1345) then
                                        v1345(v1339, v1338)
                                    elseif v1348 and not v1349 then
                                        _RERegisterHit:FireServer(v1339, v1338)
                                    end
                                end
                            else
                                return
                            end
                        else
                            return
                        end
                    else
                        return
                    end
                else
                    return
                end
            else
                return
            end
        end

        CameraShakerR = require(game.ReplicatedStorage.Util.CameraShaker)

        CameraShakerR:Stop()

        function get_Monster()
            local v1350, v1351, v1352 = pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v1353

                v1352, v1353 = v1350(v1351, v1352)

                if v1352 == nil then
                    break
                end

                local v1354 = v1353:FindFirstChild('UpperTorso') or v1353:FindFirstChild('Head')

                if v1353:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart', true) and (v1354 and (v1353.Head.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 50) then
                    return true, v1354.Position
                end
            end

            local v1355, v1356, v1357 = pairs(workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v1358

                v1357, v1358 = v1355(v1356, v1357)

                if v1357 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v1358:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and (v1358:FindFirstChild('Health') and v1358.Health.Value > 0) then
                    return true, v1358.HumanoidRootPart.Position
                end
            end

            local v1359, v1360, v1361 = pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v1362

                v1361, v1362 = v1359(v1360, v1361)

                if v1361 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v1362:FindFirstChild('Health') and (v1362.Health.Value > 0 and v1362:FindFirstChild('VehicleSeat')) then
                    return true, v1362.Engine.Position
                end
            end
        end
        function Actived()
            local _Tool = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool')
            local v1364 = next
            local v1365, v1366 = getconnections(_Tool.Activated)

            while true do
                local v1367

                v1366, v1367 = v1364(v1365, v1366)

                if v1366 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if typeof(v1367.Function) == 'function' then
                    getupvalues(v1367.Function)
                end
            end
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            RunSer.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                pcall(function()
                    if _G.Seriality then
                        AttackNoCoolDown()

                        local _Tool2 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool')
                        local _ToolTip = _Tool2.ToolTip
                        local v1370, _ = get_Monster()
                        local v1371 = _ToolTip == 'Blox Fruit' and (v1370 and _Tool2:FindFirstChild('LeftClickRemote'))

                        if v1371 then
                            Actived()
                            v1371:FireServer(Vector3.new(0.01, -500, 0.01), 1, true)
                            v1371:FireServer(false)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end)

    end
